                    np.sqrt(0.25*(1. + 1.*a) ** 2*
                    c ** 2 + (1.25 + 0.5*a + 0.25*a ** 2)*
                    x ** 2 + (1.25 - 1.25*e ** 2 + 
                    a*(0.5 - 0.5*e ** 2) + 
                    a ** 2*(0.25 - 0.25*e ** 2))*
                    y ** 2 + -0.5*(1. + 1.*a) ** 2*c*

                    x ** 2 + (1. - 1.*e ** 2)*y ** 2) ** 2))/-((1.*
                  x + (0.+1j)*np.sqrt(1. - 1.*e ** 2)*

                1.5) + -(0.5*((0.5*(2*y - 2.*e ** 2*y))/

                    1.*e ** 2*

                  np.sqrt(1. - 1.*e ** 2)*y)*
               np.sqrt(1. + (0.25*-(1.*c + 1.*a*c +
